Of the 1217, 7 are arXiv preprints bulk-imported with the GEN1_GEN2 corpus for `02_MERGED_FULL_RANKING` traceability only (not cited inline by any load-bearing claim); per SOURCE_STANDARDS.md preprints are not citable as support, so they are flagged `support_eligible:false` in sources.json and excluded from the tier-mix math below (see 99_AUDIT/FINAL_AUDIT.md §2). **Support-eligible tier mix (1210 citable sources): Tier 1: 307 (25.4%) - Tier 1+2: 950 (78.5%) - zh-language: 194.** (Raw field counts pre-exclusion: Tier1 308/Tier2 649/Tier3 260 = also >=25%/>=70%; both computations pass the gate.)
